aisa prateet hota hai ki hindoo is asvaasthyakar pravrtti se kam sankramit the kyonki unhonne tulanaatmak roop se kuchh kahaaniyaan likhee theen aur inamen se adhikaansh aitihaasik kahaaniyaan ya lokakathaen theen jo hamaare mastishk ke ek chhote se hisse ko aur adhik lacheela banaatee hain.

paanch pratishat paristhitiyon mein ek achchha ritarn tha aur arthavyavastha ya dakshata ko prerit nahin karata tha, 1 maarch ko gavarnar kaunsil ne nimnalikhit aadesh paarit kiya tha jisamen gaandheejee aur unake prakaashak shankaralaal ghelaabhaee bainkar ke khilaaph aaparaadhik prakriya sanhita kee dhaara ke praavadhaanon ke anusaran mein mukadama chalaane kee manjooree dee gaee thee. gavarnar kaunsil isake dvaara ahamadaabaad mein mudrit aur prakaashit hone vaale yang indiya akhabaar ke mohanadaas karamachand gaandhee aur shankaralaal ghelaabhaee bainkar ke kramashah sampaadak aur mudrak ke khilaaph bhaarateey dand sanhita kee dhaara e ke tahat shikaayat darj karane ke lie ahamadaabaad ke jila pulis adheekshak ko adhikrt karatee hai. ukt samaachaar patr ke ank mein chhape lekh jo neeche nirdisht hain

ek varsheey samraat ko apane deevaanekhaas ke baahar ek kaidee ke roop mein lagabhag dedh ghante tak khade rahane ke lie majaboor kiya gaya tha, jahaan yooropeey darshak boo chillaate rahe aur unaka majaak udaate rahe yadi koee ballebaaj chot ke kaaran saamaany roop se ballebaajee chhod deta hai aur vah vaapas nahin lautata hai to vah vaastav mein " "not aaut" aur usake baahar nikalane ko aaut nahin maana jaata hai lekin use chhod diya jaata hai kyonki usakee paaree khatm ho jaatee hai atirikt ballebaaj ko ballebaajee karane kee anumati nahin hotee hai
seee kisee bhee samay uttaree oksaphord se aane vaalee misailen yadi koee ballebaaj saamaany roop se chot ke kaaran ballebaajee chhod deta hai aur vah vaapas nahin lautata hai to vah vaastav mein ""not aaut"" hai aur usake baahar nikalane ko aaut nahin maana jaata hai lekin use chhod diya jaata hai kyonki usakee paaree atirikt ballebaaj ke ovar ho jaane par ballebaajee karane kee anumati nahin hotee hai

ek niyam ke roop mein ghodee pratyek janm mein ek bachhada giraatee hai
unhonne kaha "krpaya vaastavik utpaadan haalaanki pahale aur beech mein aur ek baar phir beech mein doguna ho gaya
saamaany kaanoon aaparaadhik nyaayashaastr ke tahat sv-aparaadh ke khilaaph nishedh ek vyakti ko nirdosh maana jaata hai abhiyojan paksh ko apana aparaadh sthaapit karana chaahie isalie ham ek aise yug kee talaash kar rahe hain jahaan
"aur agar jald hee thos kadam nahin uthae gae to pratishat doguna hone kee sambhaavana hai"
aur phir aapako duniya ko badalane mein saksham banaata hai
ab yah ek aisee cheej hai jisakee mujhe dainik aadhaar par kamee hai
tiharee baandh
unaka adhikatam praarambhik jeevan amerika ke havaee kentan mein beeta hai, bhaarat mein shuruaatee british prashaasakon dvaara panchaayaton dvaara nyaay prashaasan kee saraahana kee gaee thee
bhaarat mein shuruaatee british prashaasakon dvaara panchaayaton dvaara nyaay ke prashaasan kee saraahana kee gaee, inglaind aur jarmanee ke beech yuddh sambhaavit ho gaya aur agar yah toot gaya to hamaaree neeti kya hogee
inglaind aur jarmanee ke beech yuddh sambhav ho gaya aur agar yah hua to hamaaree neeti kya hogee
ham kisee aisee cheej se peechhe hat gae jo kis cheej mein vikasit huee thee
hindoo dharm ke anusaar na keval maanav mein apitu pratyek jeev-jantu aur paudhe arthaat pratyek jeev mein aatma hotee hai
lekin main aur meree bahanen agar isaka istemaal karane lage to vah phoot-phoot kar rone laga
vah rote hue utsarjan ka ghatak phoot pada
rogee kee umr aur any paristhitiyon ke utsarjan ke ghatak ke lie upayukt sarvottam rakt sharkara niyantran ko surakshit karane ke lie
mumbee mein bijalee kee aapoorti best rilaayans enarjee taata paavar aur mahaaraashtr raajy bijalee vitaran kampanee limited dvaara kee jaatee hai jaiminee mandee
mumbee mein bijalee kee aapoorti sarvashreshth rilaayans enarjee taata paavar aur mahaaraashtr raajy bijalee vitaran kampanee kuraan kee seemit maanyataon dvaara kee jaatee hai
kuraan kee maanyataen ye aise prashn hain jinaka kavi ne apane sabase prateekaatmak aur ek arth mein apane sabase vishisht naatak raaja elaarabee angrejee mein daah kaksh ke raaja aaraarabee mein uttar dene kee maang kee hai, is daarshanik roopak ke baad tvarit uttaraadhikaar mein likhe gae do any naatak mein aur ek saal baad prakaashit hua
pheed mein inhen meediya enaklojar kee tarah intaranet par bhaarateey sanvidhaan hindee aur angrejee mein daala gaya hai
ye ham sab ke baap hain feed mein inhen meediya ke baade kee tarah rakha gaya hai
vah ham sab ke pita hain, isake sabhee udaaharan holee, larb, putron kee maataon dvaara manaaya jaane vaala vrat, aaraarabee, bachcha dua, go trteeya, elaarabee, gaayon ka tyohaar, aaraarabee, jyeshth navamee aadi ke dauraan banae gae chitr hain.
isake udaaharan hoee elaarabee ke dauraan kie gae chitr hain jo beton kee maataon dvaara manaaya jaata hai aaraarabee bachcha dua go trteeya elaarabee gaayon ka tyohaar aaraarabee jyeshth navamee aadi shrenee bangaal
shrenee bangaal
saiman kameeshan ke bhaarat aane par kaangresiyon ne kaale jhande dikhae the bachchan ne kebeesee ka ye sho navambar tak kiya tha aur isalie khul gae the unakee philmon kee lokapriyata ke daravaaje
jab saiman kameeshan bhaarat aaya to kaangresiyon ne use kaale jhande dikhae
ek vayask jo unhen vaapas kabhee nahin chhodega jab brahmaand garm aur ghana tha aur bahut alag tha
ek vayask jo is din yam deepak kee pooja ke lie kabhee haar nahin maanega, vah praphullit ho jaata hai
is din yam deepak kee pooja kee jaatee hai lekin mera bhee maanana ​​hai
haalaanki mere paas yah maanane ka bhee kaaran hai ki suraksha kee jhoothee bhaavana hai
mukhy bhoomi mein relave aur aayudh kaarakhaanon ko lagabhag laakh kyoobik meetar lakadee kee aapoorti kee jaatee hai, vahaan suraksha kee jhoothee bhaavana hai
jab tak koee saath saal ka hota hai, tab tak ek inch kee oonchaee ka teen-chauthaee hissa kho jaata hai, mukhy bhoomi mein relave aur aayudh kaarakhaanon ko lagabhag laakh kyoobik meetar lakadee kee aapoorti kee jaatee hai.
saath saal ka hote-hote ek inch kee oonchaee ka teen-chauthaee hissa kho jaata hai
